<div id="header-container">
    <div id="header">
        <div id="header-menu">
            <a href="/"><div class="logo"><span></span></div></a>
            <div class="menu" style="width:503px;">
                <div class="divider"></div>

                    <div class="button">
                        <a class="unselect" id="Featured" href="/Featured"><span class="heading5a">Featured</span></a>
                    </div>
                        <div class="divider"></div>
                        <div class="button">
                            <a class="unselect" id="Originals" href="/Originals"><span class="heading5a">Originals</span></a>

                        <div class="button" id="freeShowButton" style="visibility: hidden">
                            <a class="unselect" id="FreeEpisodes" href="/FreeEpisodes"><span class="heading5a">Free Episodes</span></a>
                        </div>
                        <div class="button" id="liveStreamButton" style="visibility: hidden">
                            <a class="unselect" id="LiveTV" href="/LiveTV"><span class="heading5a">Live TV</span></a>
                        </div>
                        <div class="divider" id="freeShowDivider" style="visibility:hidden"></div>


            </div>
            <div class="search">
                <div class="search_box">
                    <input type="text" class="search_input" value="" id="searchTerm" />
                    <input type="button" class="search_button" id="btnSearch" />
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">

    var content_shared_components_submenu_branding = "starz";
    var content_session_navigation = "Featured Landing";
    var session_navigation = 'Featured';
    var logged = "False";
    var existsFreeShows = "True";
    var brand = "starz";
    var freeContentName = "Free Episodes";

    $(document).ready(function () {

        var navigation;
        userStore.set("AuthenticationFailureDefaultMessage", "We&#39;re sorry, you are not authorized to view content on STARZ Play.");
        if (session_navigation == "" && userStore != null && userStore.get('selectedTab') != "") {
            navigation = '#' + userStore.get('selectedTab');
        } else {
            navigation = '#' + session_navigation;
        }

        navigation = navigation.replace(" ", "");

        $(navigation).addClass('select');
        $(navigation).removeClass('unselect');
        $(navigation).find('span').addClass('heading5b');
        $(navigation).find('span').removeClass('heading5a');

        $('.search_input').addClass('description3aLight');

        if (logged == "False" && existsFreeShows == "True" && brand != "encore") {
            $('#freeShowButton').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#freeShowDivider').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#header-menu .menu').css('width', '670px');
        }
        if (logged == "False" && existsFreeShows == "True" && brand == "encore") {
            $('#encoreFreeShowButton').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#encoreFreeShowDivider').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#header-menu .menu').css('width', '670px');
        }

        if (logged === "True" && brand === "starz") {
            $('#freeShowButton').hide();
            $('#liveStreamButton').show();
            $('#liveStreamButton').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#freeShowDivider').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#header-menu .menu').css('width', '670px');
        } else {
            $('#liveStreamButton').hide();
        }

        return true;
    });

    function hideFreeShowButton() {
        var isLoggedIn = userStore.get('isLoggedIn');
        if (isLoggedIn && brand != "encore") {
            $('#freeShowButton').css('visibility', 'hidden');
            $('#freeShowDivider').css('visibility', 'hidden');
            if (brand != "movieplex") {
                $('#header-menu .menu').css('width', '503px');
            } else {
                $('#header-menu .menu').removeAttr('style').attr('style', 'width: 336px !important');
            }
            if (session_navigation == freeContentName) {
                window.location = window.location.protocol + '//' + window.location.host;
            }
        }
        if (isLoggedIn && brand == "encore") {
            $('#encoreFreeShowButton').css('visibility', 'hidden');
            $('#encoreFreeShowDivider').css('visibility', 'hidden');
            $('#header-menu .menu').css('width', '503px');
            if (session_navigation == freeContentName) {
                window.location = window.location.protocol + '//' + window.location.host;
            }
        }

        if (isLoggedIn && brand === 'starz') {
            $('#freeShowButton').hide();
            $('#liveStreamButton').show();
            $('#liveStreamButton').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#freeShowDivider').css('visibility', 'visible');
            $('#header-menu .menu').css('width', '670px');
        } else {
            $('#liveStreamButton').hide();
        }
    }

    $('#btnSearch').click(function () {
        goToSearch();
    });

    $('#searchTerm').keypress(function (e) {
        if (e.keyCode == 13) {
            goToSearch();
        }
    });

    function goToSearch() {
        if ($.trim(($('#searchTerm').val())) != "") {
            window.location.href = "/Search?query=" + encodeURIComponent($.trim($('#searchTerm').val()));
        }
    }

    $(function () {
        var cache = {},
			lastXhr;
        $("#searchTerm").autocomplete({
            appendTo: "div.search",
            delay: 1000,
            minLength: 1,
            position: {
                my: "left top",
                at: "left bottom",
                collision: "none",
                of: "div.search_box"
            },
            source: function (request, response) {
                var term = request.term;

                if ($.trim(term) != "") {

                    if (term in cache) {
                        hideStarzPlayer();
                        response(cache[term]);
                        hightlightSearchResults($('#searchTerm').val());
                        var results = getSearchResultCount(data);
                        playMixpanel.contentSearched($('#searchTerm').val(), results);
                        return;
                    }

                    lastXhr = $.getJSON("/Search/PredictiveSearch?query=" + encodeURIComponent($('#searchTerm').val()), request, function (data, status, xhr) {
                        cache[term] = data;
                        if (xhr === lastXhr) {
                            hideStarzPlayer();
                            response(data);
                            hightlightSearchResults($('#searchTerm').val());
                            var results = getSearchResultCount(data);
                            playMixpanel.contentSearched($('#searchTerm').val(), results);
                        }
                    });

                }
            },
            select: function (event, ui) {
                if (ui.item.link != null && ui.item.link != "") {
                    window.location.href = ui.item.link;
                }
            }
        });
    });

    function getSearchResultCount(data) {
        if (data && data.length > 0) {
            if (data[data.length - 1].label == "No Results") {
                return 0;
            }

            if (data[data.length - 1].label == "All Results") {
                return data.length - 1;
            }

            return data.length;
        }

        return 0;
    }

    function hightlightSearchResults(query) {
        query = $.trim(query);
        $('ul.ui-menu li.ui-menu-item a').each(function () {
            var text = playMixpanel.htmlDecode(this.innerHTML);
            if (text != "All Results" && text != "No Results") {
                var index = text.toLowerCase().indexOf(query.toLowerCase());
                if (index >= 0) {
                    var coloredText = "";
                    if (brand != "encore") {
                        coloredText = '<span class="description3aLight" style="word-wrap: break-word">' + text.substring(0, index) + '</span>' + '<span class="description3cLight">' + text.substring(index, index + query.length) + '</span>' + '<span class="description3aLight">' + text.substring(index + query.length) + '</span>';
                    } else {
                        coloredText = '<span class="description3aLight" style="word-wrap: break-word">' + text.substring(0, index) + '</span>' + '<span class="description3aLight" style="text-decoration: underline;">' + text.substring(index, index + query.length) + '</span>' + '<span class="description3aLight">' + text.substring(index + query.length) + '</span>';
                    }
                    this.innerHTML = coloredText;
                } else {
                    this.innerHTML = '<span class="description3aLight" style="word-wrap: break-word">' + text + '</span>';
                }
            } else {
                if (brand == "encore" && text != "No Results") {
                    this.innerHTML = '<div class="divisorLine" style="width:160px; height:1px; background-color:#FFFFFF; margin-bottom: 4px" ></div><span class="description3aLight" style="word-wrap: break-word">' + text + '</span>';
                }
            }
        });
    }

    var headerItems = $(".unselect");
    headerItems.hover(function (event) {
        $(this).find('span').addClass('header-hover');
    }, function () {
        $(this).find('span').removeClass('header-hover');
    });;

</script>

									                <table>
                                                         <tr>
                                                             <td>
                                                                <div style="width:460px;"><span class="bodyCopy3a" style="cursor:pointer;">What are the minimum system requirements for STARZ Play?</span></div>
                                                             </td>
                                                             <td>
                                                                <div class="moreInactiveButton" id="moreRelated"></div>
                                                                <div class="lessInactiveButton" id="lessRelated"></div>

								                <div class="relatedAnswer" id="relatedAnswer-000">
									                <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>A wise question. If your system does not meet the minimum requirements, you will not have the pleasurable STARZ Play experience that you should be having. Here's the criteria your computer, smart phone, tablet or other mobile device should meet before watching any of our big originals or movies.</p>
<br/><strong>Chrome Requirements</strong><br/>Google Chrome OS is now supported<br/><br/><strong>Windows Requirements</strong><br/>Microsoft Window 10, 8, 7, Vista, XP (SP2 or SP3)<br /><br/><strong>PC Browser Version</strong><br/>Microsoft Edge<br/>Internet Explorer 10.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Mac Requirements</strong><br/>Apple OSX 10.5.7 or above<br /><br/><strong>MAC Browser Version</strong><br/>Safari 6.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Computer Hardware Requirements</strong><br/>Video card with 24 bit true color and 128 MB memory<br/><br/><strong>Computer Browser Requirements</strong><br/>Flash enabled<br/>JavaScript enabled<br/>Cookies enabled<br/><br/><strong>Minimum Bandwidth</strong><br/>2.5 Mbps, but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best experience<br/>A Mobile network connection over WiFi or 4G or higher with at least 1 Mbps<br/><br/><strong>iOS (iPhone/iPad)</strong><br/>iPhone 4S, 5, 5s, 5c, 6, 6+, running iOS 7.0 or higher<br/>iPad, 2nd generation or above<br/><br/><strong>Android OS</strong><br/>Smartphones or tablets need to have Android 4.0.3 (Ice Cream Sandwich) or higher</span>

									                <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>A wise question. If your system does not meet the minimum requirements, you will not have the pleasurable STARZ Play experience that you should be having. Here's the criteria your computer, smart phone, tablet or other mobile device should meet before watching any of our big originals or movies.</p>
<br/><strong>Chrome Requirements</strong><br/>Google Chrome OS is now supported<br/><br/><strong>Windows Requirements</strong><br/>Microsoft Window 10, 8, 7, Vista, XP (SP2 or SP3)<br /><br/><strong>PC Browser Version</strong><br/>Microsoft Edge<br/>Internet Explorer 10.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Mac Requirements</strong><br/>Apple OSX 10.5.7 or above<br /><br/><strong>MAC Browser Version</strong><br/>Safari 6.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Computer Hardware Requirements</strong><br/>Video card with 24 bit true color and 128 MB memory<br/><br/><strong>Computer Browser Requirements</strong><br/>Flash enabled<br/>JavaScript enabled<br/>Cookies enabled<br/><br/><strong>Minimum Bandwidth</strong><br/>2.5 Mbps, but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best experience<br/>A Mobile network connection over WiFi or 4G or higher with at least 1 Mbps<br/><br/><strong>iOS (iPhone/iPad)</strong><br/>iPhone 4S, 5, 5s, 5c, 6, 6+, running iOS 7.0 or higher<br/>iPad, 2nd generation or above<br/><br/><strong>Android OS</strong><br/>Smartphones or tablets need to have Android 4.0.3 (Ice Cream Sandwich) or higher</span>

                                     <div class="answer" id="answer-43">
					
                                    <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>STARZ Play has titles that run the gamut, from family-friendly movies rated G, to films for adults rated NC17. There are also TV ratings like TVY (particularly suited to small children) and TVMA (unsuitable for audiences under 17). Every title on STARZ Play also comes with a detailed description page, and you'll find the rating of the show on there.
</p><p>To learn more about ratings in general visit <a href="http://mpaa.org/ratings" target="blank">http://mpaa.org/ratings</a> for movies and <a href="http://www.tvguidelines.org" target="blank">http://www.tvguidelines.org</a> for television.</p></span>

                                     <div class="answer" id="answer-70">
					
                                    <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>Is the STARZ Play application not performing correctly?&nbsp; Is playback of content bad or not playing at all?</p><p>Logging out of the app and then back in often resolves problems</p><p>Clearing the application cache can also help.</p>Android Devices:<br /><br />Select Settings<br />Select Apps<br />Select STARZ Play<br />Select Clear Data<br />Select OK<br />Restart the app and re-launch STARZ Play.

<p>Do you have any anti-virus applications installed on your Android device?&nbsp; If so, those applications could potentially block STARZ Play content.&nbsp; Please disable your anti-virus software while playing STARZ Play content for the best viewing experience!</p></span>

                                                    <div style="width:490px"><span class="bodyCopy1b" style="cursor:pointer;">The content isn&#39;t playing correctly, or the video playback is choppy.</span></div>

                                     <div class="answer" id="answer-72">
					
                                    <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>"Choppy" or stuttering video playback is often caused by a slow internet connection. The "buffering" that takes place is unable to keep up with the speed of the video playback, and as a result, the video has to keep stopping to catch up. STARZ Play can usually work around this by detecting your bandwidth and adjusting the visual quality accordingly, or by increasing the buffer. Please note that a minimum bandwidth of 2.5 Mbps is required but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best viewing experience!</p> <p>PC or Mac: If you're using a PC or Mac and the playback is still choppy, get a new video stream by closing your browser and trying again. Still no video? Then it could be a conflict with the current antivirus and firewall software installed on your machine. Check the setting of these programs to ensure they are not blocking incoming video streams from STARZ Play. And if that doesn’t solve the problem, double-check that your computer meets the minimum system requirements needed to operate STARZ Play.</p></span>
					                <div class="divisorLine" style="width:540px; height:2px; margin-top:8px; margin-left:-20px;" ></div>

Silence is not golden in this case, but there are a few steps you can take that may solve the problem. First, make sure the audio on your computer, tablet, or smart phone is working by playing something else using another website or application. If that’s working, adjust the volume on the video player, making sure that it’s not set to “mute.” Next check for any software updates to your audio card. Finally, if you’re using external speakers, check the wiring and other connections.<br /></span></p></span>

<br/><strong>Chrome Requirements</strong><br/>Google Chrome OS is now supported<br/><br/><strong>Windows Requirements</strong><br/>Microsoft Window 10, 8, 7, Vista, XP (SP2 or SP3)<br /><br/><strong>PC Browser Version</strong><br/>Microsoft Edge<br/>Internet Explorer 10.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Mac Requirements</strong><br/>Apple OSX 10.5.7 or above<br /><br/><strong>MAC Browser Version</strong><br/>Safari 6.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Computer Hardware Requirements</strong><br/>Video card with 24 bit true color and 128 MB memory<br/><br/><strong>Computer Browser Requirements</strong><br/>Flash enabled<br/>JavaScript enabled<br/>Cookies enabled<br/><br/><strong>Minimum Bandwidth</strong><br/>2.5 Mbps, but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best experience<br/>A Mobile network connection over WiFi or 4G or higher with at least 1 Mbps<br/><br/><strong>iOS (iPhone/iPad)</strong><br/>iPhone 4S, 5, 5s, 5c, 6, 6+, running iOS 7.0 or higher<br/>iPad, 2nd generation or above<br/><br/><strong>Android OS</strong><br/>Smartphones or tablets need to have Android 4.0.3 (Ice Cream Sandwich) or higher</span>

The "buffering" that takes place is unable to keep up with the speed of the video playback, and as a result, the video has to keep stopping to catch up. STARZ Play can usually work around this by detecting your bandwidth and adjusting the visual quality accordingly, or by increasing the buffer. Please note that a minimum bandwidth of 2.5 Mbps is required but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best viewing experience!</p> <p>PC or Mac: If you're using a PC or Mac and the playback is still choppy, get a new video stream by closing your browser and trying again. Still no video? Then it could be a conflict with the current antivirus and firewall software installed on your machine. Check the setting of these programs to ensure they are not blocking incoming video streams from STARZ Play. And if that doesn’t solve the problem, double-check that your computer meets the minimum system requirements needed to operate STARZ Play.</p></span>
                                                    <div class="divisorLine" style="width:510px; height:2px; margin-top:8px; margin-left:-5px;" ></div>
								                </div>
							                </div>

If your system does not meet the minimum requirements, you will not have the pleasurable STARZ Play experience that you should be having. Here's the criteria your computer, smart phone, tablet or other mobile device should meet before watching any of our big originals or movies.</p>
<br/><strong>Chrome Requirements</strong><br/>Google Chrome OS is now supported<br/><br/><strong>Windows Requirements</strong><br/>Microsoft Window 10, 8, 7, Vista, XP (SP2 or SP3)<br /><br/><strong>PC Browser Version</strong><br/>Microsoft Edge<br/>Internet Explorer 10.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Mac Requirements</strong><br/>Apple OSX 10.5.7 or above<br /><br/><strong>MAC Browser Version</strong><br/>Safari 6.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Computer Hardware Requirements</strong><br/>Video card with 24 bit true color and 128 MB memory<br/><br/><strong>Computer Browser Requirements</strong><br/>Flash enabled<br/>JavaScript enabled<br/>Cookies enabled<br/><br/><strong>Minimum Bandwidth</strong><br/>2.5 Mbps, but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best experience<br/>A Mobile network connection over WiFi or 4G or higher with at least 1 Mbps<br/><br/><strong>iOS (iPhone/iPad)</strong><br/>iPhone 4S, 5, 5s, 5c, 6, 6+, running iOS 7.0 or higher<br/>iPad, 2nd generation or above<br/><br/><strong>Android OS</strong><br/>Smartphones or tablets need to have Android 4.0.3 (Ice Cream Sandwich) or higher</span>
                                                    <div class="divisorLine" style="width:510px; height:2px; margin-top:8px; margin-left:-5px;" ></div>

								                <div class="relatedAnswer" id="relatedAnswer-780">
									                <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>"Choppy" or stuttering video playback is often caused by a slow internet connection. The "buffering" that takes place is unable to keep up with the speed of the video playback, and as a result, the video has to keep stopping to catch up. STARZ Play can usually work around this by detecting your bandwidth and adjusting the visual quality accordingly, or by increasing the buffer. Please note that a minimum bandwidth of 2.5 Mbps is required but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best viewing experience!</p> <p>PC or Mac: If you're using a PC or Mac and the playback is still choppy, get a new video stream by closing your browser and trying again. Still no video? Then it could be a conflict with the current antivirus and firewall software installed on your machine. Check the setting of these programs to ensure they are not blocking incoming video streams from STARZ Play. And if that doesn’t solve the problem, double-check that your computer meets the minimum system requirements needed to operate STARZ Play.</p></span>
                                                    <div class="divisorLine" style="width:510px; height:2px; margin-top:8px; margin-left:-5px;" ></div>

                                                    <div style="width:490px"><span class="bodyCopy1b" style="cursor:pointer;">How do I stream STARZ Play content to my Google Chromecast?</span></div>
                                                </td>

                                                    <div class="moreInactiveButton" id="moreQuestion"></div>

                                     <div class="answer" id="answer-82">
					
                                    <span class="bodyCopy3a">Launch the STARZ Play application on your Android device, Apple mobile device, or visit the STARZ Play website in your Chrome browser.  Once you are signed in to STARZ Play, select the Cast icon in the upper-right or lower-right of your browser window.  Next, select your preferred Chromecast device from the connected devices list to launch the STARZ Play application on your TV.  Select the Starz movie or show of your choice and press Play.  Because STARZ Play uses adaptive bit rate streaming, videos may appear in lower initially, but will switch to the highest possible quality after a few moments. If the video does not buffer at playback speed, the video will be downgraded to a lower quality setting, allowing for smooth playback.</span>

									                <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>Error "No Cast Devices Found" when casting from Chrome:</p><ul><li>Check to make sure you Chromecast is set up by casting other content to your TV. </li><li>Verify that your device is on the same network as your Chromecast. </li><li>Disconnect from all VPN's and proxy servers. Note that Firewall and antivirus software can prevent casting as well.</li><li>Ensure that your network is not configured as a Public network</li><li>If all else fails reboot your router, computer, and Chromecast device.</li></ul></span>

                                     <div class="answer" id="answer-84">
					
                                    <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>Error "No Cast Devices Found" when casting from Chrome:</p><ul><li>Check to make sure you Chromecast is set up by casting other content to your TV. </li><li>Verify that your device is on the same network as your Chromecast. </li><li>Disconnect from all VPN's and proxy servers. Note that Firewall and antivirus software can prevent casting as well.</li><li>Ensure that your network is not configured as a Public network</li><li>If all else fails reboot your router, computer, and Chromecast device.</li></ul></span>

                                     <div class="answer" id="answer-85">
					
                                    <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>To stop casting, simply click the cast icon from within the STARZ Play application. This will bring up a small menu with a list of connected devices. Look for the 'Disconnect' button in this window. This will not stop playback, but rather divert normal playback to back to your smartphone, tablet or Chrome browser. </p><p> If another user is also connected to the same TV, they can stop your Casting by selecting a title from their device.</p></span>

                                     <div class="answer" id="answer-91">
					
                                    <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>A wise question. If your system does not meet the minimum requirements, you will not have the pleasurable STARZ Play experience that you should be having. Here's the criteria your computer, smart phone, tablet or other mobile device should meet before watching any of our big originals or movies.</p>
<br/><strong>Chrome Requirements</strong><br/>Google Chrome OS is now supported<br/><br/><strong>Windows Requirements</strong><br/>Microsoft Window 10, 8, 7, Vista, XP (SP2 or SP3)<br /><br/><strong>PC Browser Version</strong><br/>Microsoft Edge<br/>Internet Explorer 10.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Mac Requirements</strong><br/>Apple OSX 10.5.7 or above<br /><br/><strong>MAC Browser Version</strong><br/>Safari 6.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Computer Hardware Requirements</strong><br/>Video card with 24 bit true color and 128 MB memory<br/><br/><strong>Computer Browser Requirements</strong><br/>Flash enabled<br/>JavaScript enabled<br/>Cookies enabled<br/><br/><strong>Minimum Bandwidth</strong><br/>2.5 Mbps, but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best experience<br/>A Mobile network connection over WiFi or 4G or higher with at least 1 Mbps<br/><br/><strong>iOS (iPhone/iPad)</strong><br/>iPhone 4S, 5, 5s, 5c, 6, 6+, running iOS 7.0 or higher<br/>iPad, 2nd generation or above<br/><br/><strong>Android OS</strong><br/>Smartphones or tablets need to have Android 4.0.3 (Ice Cream Sandwich) or higher</span>

                                                                <div style="width:460px;"><span class="bodyCopy3a" style="cursor:pointer;">The content isn&#39;t playing correctly, or the video playback is choppy.</span></div>

								                <div class="relatedAnswer" id="relatedAnswer-910">
									                <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>"Choppy" or stuttering video playback is often caused by a slow internet connection. The "buffering" that takes place is unable to keep up with the speed of the video playback, and as a result, the video has to keep stopping to catch up. STARZ Play can usually work around this by detecting your bandwidth and adjusting the visual quality accordingly, or by increasing the buffer. Please note that a minimum bandwidth of 2.5 Mbps is required but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best viewing experience!</p> <p>PC or Mac: If you're using a PC or Mac and the playback is still choppy, get a new video stream by closing your browser and trying again. Still no video? Then it could be a conflict with the current antivirus and firewall software installed on your machine. Check the setting of these programs to ensure they are not blocking incoming video streams from STARZ Play. And if that doesn’t solve the problem, double-check that your computer meets the minimum system requirements needed to operate STARZ Play.</p></span>
                                                    <div class="divisorLine" style="width:510px; height:2px; margin-top:8px; margin-left:-5px;" ></div>

If that’s working, adjust the volume on the video player, making sure that it’s not set to “mute.” Next check for any software updates to your audio card. Finally, if you’re using external speakers, check the wiring and other connections.<br /></span></p></span>

<br/><strong>Chrome Requirements</strong><br/>Google Chrome OS is now supported<br/><br/><strong>Windows Requirements</strong><br/>Microsoft Window 10, 8, 7, Vista, XP (SP2 or SP3)<br /><br/><strong>PC Browser Version</strong><br/>Microsoft Edge<br/>Internet Explorer 10.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Mac Requirements</strong><br/>Apple OSX 10.5.7 or above<br /><br/><strong>MAC Browser Version</strong><br/>Safari 6.0 or higher<br/>Chrome 30.0 or higher<br/>Firefox 30.0 or higher<br/><br/><strong>Computer Hardware Requirements</strong><br/>Video card with 24 bit true color and 128 MB memory<br/><br/><strong>Computer Browser Requirements</strong><br/>Flash enabled<br/>JavaScript enabled<br/>Cookies enabled<br/><br/><strong>Minimum Bandwidth</strong><br/>2.5 Mbps, but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best experience<br/>A Mobile network connection over WiFi or 4G or higher with at least 1 Mbps<br/><br/><strong>iOS (iPhone/iPad)</strong><br/>iPhone 4S, 5, 5s, 5c, 6, 6+, running iOS 7.0 or higher<br/>iPad, 2nd generation or above<br/><br/><strong>Android OS</strong><br/>Smartphones or tablets need to have Android 4.0.3 (Ice Cream Sandwich) or higher</span>
                                                    <div class="divisorLine" style="width:510px; height:2px; margin-top:8px; margin-left:-5px;" ></div>

								                <div class="relatedAnswer" id="relatedAnswer-930">
									                <span class="bodyCopy3a"><p>"Choppy" or stuttering video playback is often caused by a slow internet connection. The "buffering" that takes place is unable to keep up with the speed of the video playback, and as a result, the video has to keep stopping to catch up. STARZ Play can usually work around this by detecting your bandwidth and adjusting the visual quality accordingly, or by increasing the buffer. Please note that a minimum bandwidth of 2.5 Mbps is required but we recommend 6 Mbps for the best viewing experience!</p> <p>PC or Mac: If you're using a PC or Mac and the playback is still choppy, get a new video stream by closing your browser and trying again. Still no video? Then it could be a conflict with the current antivirus and firewall software installed on your machine. Check the setting of these programs to ensure they are not blocking incoming video streams from STARZ Play. And if that doesn’t solve the problem, double-check that your computer meets the minimum system requirements needed to operate STARZ Play.</p></span>

<h3>
   <strong>PRIVACY POLICY</strong>
</h3>
<p>
    IMPORTANT! PLEASE READ THIS PRIVACY POLICY (<strong>"PRIVACY POLICY"</strong>) CAREFULLY. THIS PRIVACY POLICY APPLIES TO YOUR USE OF STARZ ENTERTAINMENT,
    LLC'S (<strong>"STARZ," "US" or "WE"</strong>): (1) STARZ PLAY, ENCORE PLAY AND MOVIEPLEX PLAY SERVICES (<strong>"SERVICES"</strong>); (2) WEBSITES LOCATED
    AT STARZPLAY.COM, ENCOREPLAY.COM AND MOVIEPLEXPLAY.COM ASSOCIATED WITH THE SERVICES (<strong>"SITES"</strong>); AND (3) INTERACTIVE FEATURES OR DOWNLOADS THAT
    ARE MADE AVAILABLE THROUGH OR INTERACT WITH THE SERVICES OR SITES (<strong>"FEATURES"</strong>). By USING THE SERVICES, SITES OR FEATURES YOU ARE
    UNCONDITIONALLY AGREEING TO THIS PRIVACY POLICY. IF YOU DO NOT AGREE TO THE TERMS OF THIS PRIVACY POLICY, PLEASE DO NOT USE THE SERVICES OR THE SITES.
</p>
<p>
    Starz is committed to helping users of its Services, Sites and Features understand the information that Starz collects, how Starz uses that information,
    the choices users have about the way their information is used, and the precautions Starz takes to protect information concerning its users. This Privacy
    Policy applies specifically to the Services, Sites and Features only, and covers information collected on or through the Services, Sites and Features. When
    using other Starz web sites, we encourage you to review the privacy policy controlling that particular site.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>1. Information We Collect.</strong>
</p>
<p>
    a. <strong>Personally Identifiable Information.</strong> Starz collects personally identifiable information that you voluntarily submit in various contexts
    including, but not limited to: (1) the registration or account creation process for the Services; (2) the registration process for sweepstakes, contests,
    Features and other promotions offered via the Services and Sites; (3) your participation in online research surveys offered on the Services, Sites and
    Features; (4) the process of reporting a problem with our Services, Sites and Features and resolving customer service activities (including via email and
    chat), and (5) in connection with content submissions, voting and polling activities. Such personally identifiable information may include, without
    limitation, name, date of birth, e-mail address, mailing address and telephone number.
</p>
<p>
    This Privacy Policy does not apply to any personally identifiable information you may disclose in public areas of the Services, Sites and Features. When
    you voluntarily post information in public areas of the Services, Sites and Features, that information can be collected and used by third parties. Starz
    assumes no responsibility for any action or policies of any third parties who collect information that users disclose on public areas of the Services,
    Sites and Features.
</p>
<p>
    b. <strong>Non-personally Identifiable Information.</strong>
</p>
<p>
    (i) <u>Usage Information</u>. When you visit the Services, Sites and Features, Starz may also collect non-personally identifiable information. Starz may
    automatically collect information that describes how you use the Services, Sites and Features and the technology you are using to access the Services,
    Sites and Features (<strong>"Usage Information"</strong>). Additionally, we may collect your IP address or device identifier (<strong>"Device ID"</strong>
    ). A Device ID is a unique number assigned to the device(s) or network you use to access the Services, Sites and Features. If we associate Usage
    Information with your Device ID we will treat such information as personally identifiable information.
</p>
<p>
    (ii) <u>Cookies</u>. Cookies are small information files that our Services, Sites and Features may place on your computer or other device. Cookies by
    themselves do not provide Starz with personally identifiable information. However, once you choose to furnish us with personally identifiable information,
    this information may be linked to the data stored in a cookie. In many instances you can turn off cookies in your web browser (see your browser's manual or
    help file for instructions), but if you do turn off cookies you may not be able to access parts of the Services, Sites and Features where cookies are used.
</p>
<p>
    (iii) <u>Embedded Scripts/Web Beacons</u>. An embedded script is programming code used to collect information about how you interact with the Services,
    Sites and Features. The embedded script is temporarily downloaded onto your device from a Starz or third party web server and is active only while you are
    connected to the Services, Sites and Features. A web beacon is a small graphic image or programming code that may be included in our web pages and e-mail
    messages.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>2. How We Use the Information We Collect. </strong>
</p>
<p>
a. <strong>Personally Identifiable Information.</strong> We use the personally identifiable you give us to deliver information or content you    <a name="_GoBack"></a>request, to contact you about the Services, Sites and Features, or for other purposes explained at the time we collect the
    information. Additionally, we use personally identifiable information to, among other things: (1) verify access rights to the Services, Sites and Features;
    (2) verifying the status of your User Account (as defined in the Terms of Use for the Services and Sites); (3) improve the Services, Sites and Features by
    providing personalized content, language and location customization and/or personalized help and instructions; (4) provide customer service assistance; (5)
    ask you to participate in surveys about products, services, news and events; (6) provide you with news, newsletters, updates, targeted advertising,
    promotions, sweepstakes and special offers; (7) better understand how the Services, Sites and Features are used, including traffic patterns and what types
    of content are most popular with users; (8) in connection with content submissions, community postings (e.g., chat and bulletin boards), and voting and
    polling activities.
</p>
<p>
    b. <strong>Non-personally Identifiable Information.</strong> We use Device IDs, Usage Information, cookies and web beacons for a variety of internal
    purposes, such as system administration and counting visitors, tracking views, email "opens" and monitoring how users navigate the Services, Sites and
    Features.
</p>
<p>
    Starz may disclose personally identifiable information and non-personally identifiable information to distributors, contractors and third party agents we
    engage to provide services for Starz. Such entities and individuals are required to protect your personally identifiable information in a manner that is
    consistent with this Privacy Policy and to not use such personal information for any purpose other than to carry out the services they are performing for
    Starz.
</p>
<p>
    Starz may disclose your personally identifiable information and non-personally identifiable information to any successor or to any person or entity that
    acquires ownership or control of the Services, Sites and Features by any means. You hereby consent to the disclosure to, and use by, any such successor or
    subsequent owner or operator, and your continued use of the Services, Sites and Features signifies your agreement to be bound by such successor's or
    subsequent owner or operator's own privacy policy. Starz is not responsible for any changes or modifications to this Privacy Policy by any successor or
    subsequent owner or operator of the Services, Sites and Features.
</p>
<p>
    Starz may also disclose your personally identifiable information to third parties in any of the following instances: 1) we have been given your consent to
    disclose; 2) we have previously informed you of the disclosure, including by means of our Privacy Policy; 3) we are required by law or court order to
    disclose, or we believe in good faith that the law requires it; 4) disclosure is necessary to identify, contact, or bring legal action against, someone who
    may cause or be causing harm to, or interference with, our rights or property, other users of the Services, Sites and Features, or anyone else; or 5) to
    respond to an inquiry, request or complaint that you have made. We may also use IP addresses in cooperation with Internet service providers to identify
    users if we deem it necessary to comply with laws, to enforce compliance with the Privacy Policy.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>3. </strong>
    <strong>How To Update Your Personal Information. </strong>
    We will use reasonable efforts to allow you to update or correct personally identifiable information, to the extent that changing the data will not
    compromise privacy or security interests. Also, upon your request, we will use commercially reasonable efforts to functionally delete your personally
    identifiable information from our database. However, it may be impossible to delete all of your information without some residual data because of backups
    and records of deletions. You can access and update the personally identifiable information that you have provided in connection with the Services, Sites
    and Features by visiting the My Account tool available within the Services. To help protect your privacy and security, we will take reasonable steps to
    verify your identity before granting access or making corrections to any personally identifiable information.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>4. EMAIL OPT-OUT.</strong>
    If at any time you wish to opt out or "unsubscribe" from receiving commercial emails related to the Services, Sites and Features you may: (a) use the
    unsubscribe link at the bottom of each commercial e-mail you receive; or (b) visit the My Account tool available within the Services to opt out of
    receiving commercial e-mails and to update your email preferences. Please remember that: (1) even if you opt out of receiving commercial emails from Starz,
    we reserve the right to send transactional or relationship communications to you (e.g., if we need to contact you regarding your account status, technical
    support, product information, changes to the terms of use for the Services, Sites and Features or this Privacy Policy, and any other matter that might
    affect our service to you and/or our records on you); and (2) certain information or services can only be provided to you if personal information is
    provided. If you elect not to provide such information or opt out of having your information shared, you may not be able to receive certain content or
    information.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>5.</strong>
    <strong>Policies for Individuals Under the Age of 13. </strong>
    Starz does not knowingly collect or use any personally identifiable information submitted to the Service, Sites and/or Features from individuals under the
    age of 13, except in order to respond on a one-time basis to a specific request for information. If you are a parent or guardian who has discovered that
    your child under the age of 13 has submitted his or her personally identifiable information without your permission or consent, you can ask us to remove
    your child's information by contacting us at <a href="mailto:business.affairs@starz.com">business.affairs@starz.com</a>. Upon notice from you, Starz will
    make reasonable efforts to investigate and remove the information. Please include in your message the same user name and/or e-mail address and password
    that your child submitted.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>6. Links to Other Sites. </strong>
    Starz may from time to time offer links to other sites from the Services, Sites and Features, including the sites of our distributors and sites that are
    sponsored by or co-branded with third parties. These third parties may have information practices that are different than ours. We recommend that you
    review such site's terms of use and privacy policy prior to use or submitting any personally identifiable information. Starz does not verify, warrant,
    endorse or take responsibility for the availability, accuracy, completeness, quality, practices or policies of such sites or content available from such
    sites. Starz does not make any representations or warranties as to the security of any information (including, without limitation, credit card and other
    personal information) you might be requested to give any third party, and you irrevocably waive any claim against us with respect to such sites.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>7. Starz Security Policy. </strong>
    Starz is aware of your privacy concerns and strives to collect only as much data as is required to make your use of the Services, Sites and Features as
    efficient and satisfying as possible, in the most unobtrusive manner as possible. We will make reasonable efforts to ensure that whatever information you
    provide will be maintained in a secure environment. Unfortunately, no data transmission over the Internet can be guaranteed to be 100% secure. As a result,
    while we strive to protect your personally identifiable information, we cannot guarantee the security of any information you transmit to us or from our
    products or services, and you provide such information at your own risk.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>8. Consent to Processing in the United States. </strong>
    By providing any personally identifiable information to Starz, all users, including, without limitation, users in the member states of the European Union,
    fully understand and unambiguously consent to this Privacy Policy and to the collection and processing of such information in the United States of America.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>9. Notification of Changes.</strong>
    <strong> </strong>

<p>

<p>

    function configurePlayerAnalytics(bridge) {
        if(bridge !=null){
            try{
                bridge.setProperty("omniture.tracking.server", "deluxedigitalstudios.112.2o7.net");
                bridge.setProperty("omniture.account", "ddsd3starztest");
                bridge.setProperty("omniture.visitor.namespace", "deluxedigitalstudios");
                bridge.setProperty("omniture.page.name", "Video Player");
                bridge.setProperty("omniture.device", deviceId);
                bridge.setProperty("omniture.deviceType", "Web");

                bridge.setProperty("omniture.buildNumber", BuildNumber);
                bridge.setProperty("omniture.userVersion", UserVersion);

                bridge.setProperty("conviva.customer.id", "c3.Starz");
                bridge.setProperty("conviva.service.url", "http://livepass.conviva.com");
                bridge.setProperty("conviva.enabled", "True");

                if (userSessionValuesIsLoggedIn) {
                    bridge.setProperty("omniture.distributor", playMixpanel.getDistributorNameFromStore());
                    bridge.setProperty("omniture.islogged", "Yes");
                    bridge.setProperty("omniture.user", userSessionValuesUserId);
                } else {
                    bridge.setProperty("omniture.distributor", "No Distributor");
                    bridge.setProperty("omniture.islogged", "No");
                    bridge.setProperty("omniture.user", "Anonymous");
                }

                bridge.setProperty("digital.locker.url", "https://stapi.dmlib.com/v2/");
                bridge.setProperty("dl.api.key", "9249F0EE-460F-E7CF-E356-38A50D23AA31");
                bridge.setProperty("ajax.url.prefix", ajaxUrlPrefix);

                bridge.configureAnalytics();
            } catch(err){
            }
        }
    }

    if (window.name == "logged") {
        window.name = "none";
        if (!userSessionValuesIsLoggedIn) {
            location.reload();
        }
    } else if (window.name == "unlogged") {
        window.name = "none";
        if (userSessionValuesIsLoggedIn) {
            location.reload();
        }
    }
